   TrustManagerFactory.SunX509 -> sun.security.ssl.TrustManagerFactoryImpl$SimpleFactory
   XMLSignatureFactory.DOM -> org.jcp.xml.dsig.internal.dom.DOMXMLSignatureFactory

    public static void storeProperties(java.lang.String outFile, java.util.Properties props, java.lang.String message) throws java.lang.Exception {

                outFile = args[i + 1];

        }

        if (outFile == null) {
            java.lang.System.out.println("You must specify an input file or output file");
            java.lang.System.exit(1);
        }
        java.util.Properties props = org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.EncryptedPropertiesUtils.loadProperties(inFile, inFileEncrypted);

        do {
            java.lang.System.out.print("Enter key: ");
            key = br.readLine();

                java.lang.System.out.print("Key already exists. Replace? ");
                java.lang.String confirm = br.readLine();
                if (!("y".equals(confirm) || "yes".equals(confirm))) {
                    continue;
                }
            }
            java.lang.System.out.print("Enter value: ");

                java.lang.String value = props.getProperty(sKey);
                java.lang.System.out.println((("   " + sKey) + "=") + value);
            }
        }
    }

    public static java.util.Properties loadProperties(java.lang.String inFile, java.lang.Boolean inFileEncrypted) throws java.io.IOException {
        if (inFileEncrypted == null) {
            inFileEncrypted = true;
        }
        java.util.Properties props;

            java.io.File f = new java.io.File(inFile);

                spoonDefaultValue = true;
            } catch (java.lang.Exception __NopolProcessorException) {
            }

                try{fr.inria.lille.commons.trace.RuntimeValues.instance(13).collectInput("inFile",inFile);} catch (Exception ex1) {ex1.printStackTrace();};
                try{fr.inria.lille.commons.trace.RuntimeValues.instance(13).collectInput("f",f);} catch (Exception ex1) {ex1.printStackTrace();};
                fr.inria.lille.commons.trace.RuntimeValues.instance(13).collectOutput(runtimeAngelicValue);
                fr.inria.lille.commons.trace.RuntimeValues.instance(13).collectionEnds();
            }
            if (runtimeAngelicValue) if (!f.exists()) {
                java.lang.System.out.println("Input properties file not found. Creating new.");
                props = new org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.ReferenceEncryptedProperties();
            } else {
                java.lang.String encrypted = (inFileEncrypted) ? "Encrypted" : "Plaintext";
                java.lang.System.out.println((encrypted + " properties found in ") + f.getAbsolutePath());
                java.util.Properties inProperties;
                if (inFileEncrypted) {
                    inProperties = new org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.ReferenceEncryptedProperties();
                } else {
                    inProperties = new java.util.Properties();
                }
                java.io.InputStream in = null;
                try {
                    in = new java.io.FileInputStream(f);
                    inProperties.load(in);
                } finally {
                    try {
                        if (in != null) {
                            in.close();
                        }
                    } catch (java.lang.Exception e) {
                    }
                }
                props = new org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.ReferenceEncryptedProperties(inProperties);
            }
        } else {
            java.lang.System.out.println("Input properties file not found. Creating new.");
            props = new org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.ReferenceEncryptedProperties();
        }
        return props;
    }

    public static void storeProperties(java.lang.String outFile, java.util.Properties props, java.lang.String message) throws java.lang.Exception {
        java.io.OutputStream out = null;
        try {
            out = new java.io.FileOutputStream(new java.io.File(outFile));
            props.store(out, message);
        } finally {
            try {
                if (out != null) {
                    out.close();
                }
            } catch (java.lang.Exception e) {
            }
        }
    }

    public static java.lang.Object addProperty(java.util.Properties props, java.lang.String key, java.lang.String value) {
        if (((((props != null) && (key != null)) && (key.length() > 0)) && (value != null)) && (value.length() > 0)) {
            return props.setProperty(key, value);
        }
        return null;
    }

public class EncryptedPropertiesUtils {
    public static void main(java.lang.String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception {
        java.lang.String inFile = null;
        java.lang.String outFile = null;
        boolean inFileEncrypted = true;
        boolean verbose = false;
        for (int i = 0; i < args.length; i = i + 2) {
            java.lang.String paramType = args[i];
            if ("--in".equals(paramType) && (args.length >= (i + 1))) {
                inFile = args[i + 1];
            } else if ("--out".equals(paramType) && (args.length >= (i + 1))) {
                outFile = args[i + 1];
            } else if ("--in-encrypted".equals(paramType) && (args.length >= (i + 1))) {
                inFileEncrypted = java.lang.Boolean.valueOf(args[i + 1]);
            } else if ("--verbose".equals(paramType) && (args.length >= (i + 1))) {
                verbose = java.lang.Boolean.valueOf(args[i + 1]);
            }
        }
        if (outFile == null) {
            outFile = inFile;
        }
        if (outFile == null) {
            java.lang.System.out.println("You must specify an input file or output file");
            java.lang.System.exit(1);
        }
        java.util.Properties props = org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.EncryptedPropertiesUtils.loadProperties(inFile, inFileEncrypted);
        java.io.BufferedReader br = new java.io.BufferedReader(new java.io.InputStreamReader(java.lang.System.in));
        java.lang.String key = null;
        do {
            java.lang.System.out.print("Enter key: ");
            key = br.readLine();
            if (props.containsKey(key)) {
                java.lang.System.out.print("Key already exists. Replace? ");
                java.lang.String confirm = br.readLine();
                if (!("y".equals(confirm) || "yes".equals(confirm))) {
                    continue;
                }
            }
            java.lang.System.out.print("Enter value: ");
            java.lang.String value = br.readLine();
            org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.EncryptedPropertiesUtils.addProperty(props, key, value);
        } while ((key != null) && (key.length() > 0) );
        org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.EncryptedPropertiesUtils.storeProperties(outFile, props, "Encrypted Properties File generated by org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.EncryptedPropertiesUtils");
        java.lang.System.out.println("Encrypted Properties file output to " + outFile);
        if (verbose) {
            for (java.lang.Object oKey : props.keySet()) {
                java.lang.String sKey = ((java.lang.String) (oKey));
                java.lang.String value = props.getProperty(sKey);
                java.lang.System.out.println((("   " + sKey) + "=") + value);
            }
        }
    }

    public static java.util.Properties loadProperties(java.lang.String inFile, java.lang.Boolean inFileEncrypted) throws java.io.IOException {
        if (inFileEncrypted == null) {
            inFileEncrypted = true;
        }
        java.util.Properties props;
        if (inFile != null) {
            java.io.File f = new java.io.File(inFile);
            if (!f.exists()) {
                java.lang.System.out.println("Input properties file not found. Creating new.");
                props = new org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.ReferenceEncryptedProperties();
            } else {
                java.lang.String encrypted = (inFileEncrypted) ? "Encrypted" : "Plaintext";
                java.lang.System.out.println((encrypted + " properties found in ") + f.getAbsolutePath());
                java.util.Properties inProperties;
                if (inFileEncrypted) {
                    inProperties = new org.owasp.esapi.reference.crypto.ReferenceEncryptedProperties();
                } else {

    public byte[] asSerializedByteArray() {
        int kdfInfo = cipherText_.getKDFInfo();
        debug("asSerializedByteArray: kdfInfo = " + kdfInfo);

        java.lang.String cipherXform = cipherText_.getCipherTransformation();
        assert cipherText_.getKeySize() < java.lang.Short.MAX_VALUE : "Key size too large. Max is " + java.lang.Short.MAX_VALUE;

    private byte[] computeSerialization(int kdfInfo, long timestamp, java.lang.String cipherXform, short keySize, short blockSize, short ivLen, byte[] iv, int ciphertextLen, byte[] rawCiphertext, short macLen, byte[] mac) {
        debug("computeSerialization: kdfInfo = " + kdfInfo);
        debug("computeSerialization: timestamp = " + new java.util.Date(timestamp));
        debug("computeSerialization: cipherXform = " + cipherXform);
        debug("computeSerialization: keySize = " + keySize);
        debug("computeSerialization: blockSize = " + blockSize);
        debug("computeSerialization: ivLen = " + ivLen);
        debug("computeSerialization: ciphertextLen = " + ciphertextLen);
        debug("computeSerialization: macLen = " + macLen);
        java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream baos = new java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream();
        writeInt(baos, kdfInfo);
        writeLong(baos, timestamp);
        java.lang.String[] parts = cipherXform.split("/");
        assert parts.length == 3 : "Malformed cipher transformation";
        writeString(baos, cipherXform);
        writeShort(baos, keySize);
        writeShort(baos, blockSize);
        writeShort(baos, ivLen);
        if (ivLen > 0) {
            baos.write(iv, 0, iv.length);
        }
        writeInt(baos, ciphertextLen);
        baos.write(rawCiphertext, 0, rawCiphertext.length);
        writeShort(baos, macLen);
        if (macLen > 0) {
            baos.write(mac, 0, mac.length);
        }
        return baos.toByteArray();
    }

    private java.lang.String readString(java.io.ByteArrayInputStream bais, short sz) throws java.lang.NullPointerException, java.io.IOException {
        byte[] bytes = new byte[sz];
        int ret = bais.read(bytes, 0, sz);
        assert ret == sz : ("readString: Failed to read " + sz) + " bytes.";
        return new java.lang.String(bytes, "UTF8");
    }

    private void writeShort(java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream baos, short s) {
        byte[] shortAsByteArray = org.owasp.esapi.util.ByteConversionUtil.fromShort(s);
        assert shortAsByteArray.length == 2;
        baos.write(shortAsByteArray, 0, 2);
    }

    private short readShort(java.io.ByteArrayInputStream bais) throws java.lang.NullPointerException, java.lang.IndexOutOfBoundsException {
        byte[] shortAsByteArray = new byte[2];
        int ret = bais.read(shortAsByteArray, 0, 2);
        assert ret == 2 : "readShort: Failed to read 2 bytes.";
        return org.owasp.esapi.util.ByteConversionUtil.toShort(shortAsByteArray);
    }

    private void writeInt(java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream baos, int i) {
        byte[] intAsByteArray = org.owasp.esapi.util.ByteConversionUtil.fromInt(i);
        baos.write(intAsByteArray, 0, 4);
    }

    private int readInt(java.io.ByteArrayInputStream bais) throws java.lang.NullPointerException, java.lang.IndexOutOfBoundsException {

        assert ret == 4 : "readInt: Failed to read 4 bytes.";
        return org.owasp.esapi.util.ByteConversionUtil.toInt(intAsByteArray);
    }

    private void writeLong(java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream baos, long l) {

        assert longAsByteArray.length == 8;
        baos.write(longAsByteArray, 0, 8);
    }

        return org.owasp.esapi.util.ByteConversionUtil.toLong(longAsByteArray);
    }

    private org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherText convertToCipherText(byte[] cipherTextSerializedBytes) throws org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException {
        try {
            assert cipherTextSerializedBytes != null : "cipherTextSerializedBytes cannot be null.";
            assert cipherTextSerializedBytes.length > 0 : "cipherTextSerializedBytes must be > 0 in length.";
            java.io.ByteArrayInputStream bais = new java.io.ByteArrayInputStream(cipherTextSerializedBytes);
            int kdfInfo = readInt(bais);
            debug("kdfInfo: " + kdfInfo);
            int kdfPrf = kdfInfo >>> 28;
            debug("kdfPrf: " + kdfPrf);
            assert (kdfPrf >= 0) && (kdfPrf <= 15) : ("kdfPrf == " + kdfPrf) + " must be between 0 and 15.";
            int kdfVers = kdfInfo & 0x7ffffff;
            if (!org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CryptoHelper.isValidKDFVersion(kdfVers, false, false)) {
                java.lang.String logMsg = ((((("KDF version read from serialized ciphertext (" + kdfVers) + ") is out of range. ") + "Valid range for KDF version is [") + org.owasp.esapi.crypto.KeyDerivationFunction.originalVersion) + ", ") + "99991231].";
                throw new org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException("Version info from serialized ciphertext not in valid range.", "Likely tampering with KDF version on serialized ciphertext." + logMsg);
            }
            debug((("convertToCipherText: kdfPrf = " + kdfPrf) + ", kdfVers = ") + kdfVers);
            if (!org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherTextSerializer.versionIsCompatible(kdfVers)) {
                throw new org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException("This version of ESAPI is not compatible with the version of ESAPI that encrypted your data.", (("KDF version " + kdfVers) + " from serialized ciphertext not compatibile with current KDF version of ") + org.owasp.esapi.crypto.KeyDerivationFunction.kdfVersion);
            }
            long timestamp = readLong(bais);
            debug("convertToCipherText: timestamp = " + new java.util.Date(timestamp));
            short strSize = readShort(bais);
            debug("convertToCipherText: length of cipherXform = " + strSize);
            java.lang.String cipherXform = readString(bais, strSize);
            debug("convertToCipherText: cipherXform = " + cipherXform);
            java.lang.String[] parts = cipherXform.split("/");
            assert parts.length == 3 : "Malformed cipher transformation";
            java.lang.String cipherMode = parts[1];
            if (!org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CryptoHelper.isAllowedCipherMode(cipherMode)) {
                java.lang.String msg = ("Cipher mode " + cipherMode) + " is not an allowed cipher mode";
                throw new org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException(msg, msg);
            }
            short keySize = readShort(bais);
            debug("convertToCipherText: keySize = " + keySize);
            short blockSize = readShort(bais);
            debug("convertToCipherText: blockSize = " + blockSize);
            short ivLen = readShort(bais);
            debug("convertToCipherText: ivLen = " + ivLen);
            byte[] iv = null;
            if (ivLen > 0) {
                iv = new byte[ivLen];
                bais.read(iv, 0, iv.length);
            }
            int ciphertextLen = readInt(bais);
            debug("convertToCipherText: ciphertextLen = " + ciphertextLen);
            assert ciphertextLen > 0 : "convertToCipherText: Invalid cipher text length";
            byte[] rawCiphertext = new byte[ciphertextLen];
            bais.read(rawCiphertext, 0, rawCiphertext.length);
            short macLen = readShort(bais);
            debug("convertToCipherText: macLen = " + macLen);
            byte[] mac = null;
            if (macLen > 0) {
                mac = new byte[macLen];
                bais.read(mac, 0, mac.length);
            }
            org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherSpec cipherSpec = new org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherSpec(cipherXform, keySize);
            cipherSpec.setBlockSize(blockSize);
            cipherSpec.setIV(iv);
            debug("convertToCipherText: CipherSpec: " + cipherSpec);
            org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherText ct = new org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherText(cipherSpec);
            if (!((ivLen > 0) && ct.requiresIV())) {
                throw new org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException("convertToCipherText: Mismatch between IV length and cipher mode.", "Possible tampering of serialized ciphertext?");
            }
            ct.setCiphertext(rawCiphertext);
            ct.setEncryptionTimestamp(timestamp);
            if (macLen > 0) {
                ct.storeSeparateMAC(mac);
            }
            ct.setKDF_PRF(kdfPrf);
            ct.setKDFVersion(kdfVers);
            return ct;
        } catch (org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException ex) {
            throw new org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException("Cannot deserialize byte array into CipherText object", "Cannot deserialize byte array into CipherText object", ex);
        } catch (java.io.IOException e) {
            throw new org.owasp.esapi.errors.EncryptionException("Cannot deserialize byte array into CipherText object", "Cannot deserialize byte array into CipherText object", e);
        }
    }

    private static boolean versionIsCompatible(int readKdfVers) {
        assert readKdfVers > 0 : "Extracted KDF version is negative!";
        switch (readKdfVers) {
            case org.owasp.esapi.crypto.KeyDerivationFunction.originalVersion :
                return true;
            case org.owasp.esapi.crypto.KeyDerivationFunction.kdfVersion :
                return true;
            default :
                return false;
        }
    }

    private void debug(java.lang.String msg) {
        if (org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherTextSerializer.logger.isDebugEnabled()) {
            org.owasp.esapi.crypto.CipherTextSerializer.logger.debug(org.owasp.esapi.Logger.EVENT_SUCCESS, msg);
        }
    }
}
